    <script type="text/javascript">

        function showLogout()
        {
            $ ('#logout').show();
        }

        function hideLogout()
        {
            $ ('#logout').hide();
        }

        function confirmLogout()
        {
            var link = $('#logoutLink').attr('logout-url');
            if (link) {
                document.location=link;
            }
        }

    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function enableChangePlatform() {
        var element = $('#changePlatform');
        if (element.data('onclick')) {
            element.attr('onclick', element.data('onclick'));
        }
    }

    if (typeof (chipVersion131) != "function") {
        document.addEventListener('jQueryReady', function () {
            $ ("head").append ("<link rel='stylesheet' type='text/css' href='https://static.jobs.bg/mobile/assets/css/chips.5329c061a5f363bc2ff6.css' />");
            $.getScript ("https://static.jobs.bg/mobile/assets/js/chips.c2c63c62b8de00f10844.js", function () {
                enableChangePlatform();

                initChips();
                            });
            document.removeEventListener('jQueryReady', arguments.callee);
        });
    }
    else {
        $( document ).ready(function() {
            enableChangePlatform();

            initChips();
                    });
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

    function deleteSHConfirm()
    {
        closeSearchHistoryDeletePopup();
        var postData = 'csrf_token=' + $('.page.active .fav-popup input[name="csrf_token"]').val() + '&' + $("#searchHistoryPageList input").serialize();

        $.ajax ({
            type: "POST",
            url: "https://www.jobs.bg/search_history.php",
            data: postData,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (response) {

                if (response.error && response.error == 'csrf') {
                    $('#csrfErrorModal').show();
                    if (response.csrf) {
                        $('#listPage input[name="csrf_token"]').val(response.csrf);
                    }
                }
                else {
                    loadSearchHistorySheet();
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function openSearchHistoryDeletePopup ()
    {
        $ ('#searchHistoryDeletePopup').show ();
    }

    function closeSearchHistoryDeletePopup ()
    {
        $ ('#searchHistoryDeletePopup').hide ();
    }

    function openSearchHistorySheet()
    {
        loadSearchHistorySheet();
        $('#searchHistorySheet').addClass('bottom-sheet-show');
        $('html').addClass('scroll-lock');

        $('#searchHistorySheet button').first().focus();
    }

    function loadSearchHistorySheet()
    {
        $("#searchHistorySheetContainer").html('').css('background-size', '32px 32px');
        $.ajax ({
            type: "POST",
            url: "https://www.jobs.bg/search_history.php",
            data: 'load=1',
            success: function (result) {
                $("#searchHistorySheetContainer").css('background-size', '0 0').html(result);

                if ($('.mdc-switch').length) {
                    mdc.InitComponentFirst('#searchHistorySheetContainer .mdc-switch', 'MDCSwitch');
                }

                if ($('#searchHistoryPageList').length) {
                    $('#deleteSearchHistoryLink').show();
                }
                else {
                    $('#deleteSearchHistoryLink').hide();
                    if ($('#turnOnSearchHistorySwitch').length) {
                        $('.quicklinks-couter-text').html('(изключено)');
                    }
                    else {
                        $('.quicklinks-couter-text').html('');
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>	
<div class="fav-popup" style="display: none;">
            <div id="fav-popup-dialog" class="mdc-dialog mdc-dialog--open ">
            <div class="mdc-dialog__container">
                <div class="mdc-dialog__surface" role="alertdialog" aria-modal="true" aria-labelledby="fav-popup-dialog-title" aria-describedby="fav-popup-dialog-content">
                    <div class="mdc-dialog__content" id="fav-popup-dialog-content">
                Искате ли да имате възможност да повтаряте предишни търсения и предпочитания като категории, населени места и др.?            </div>
                    <div class="mdc-dialog__actions">
            <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="JKvf8bLtDxD0zgoW3_xNjJ4hQNWUBBpzR3GFX6DT054" autocomplete="off">    <button onclick="favConfirm (0);" type="button" class="mdc-button mdc-dialog__button" data-mdc-dialog-action="cancel">
        <div class="mdc-button__ripple"></div>
        <span class="mdc-button__label">Не</span>
    </button>
    <button onclick="favConfirm (1);" type="button" class="mdc-button mdc-dialog__button" data-mdc-dialog-action="discard">
        <div class="mdc-button__ripple"></div>
        <span class="mdc-button__label">Да</span>
    </button>
            </div>
                            </div>
            </div>
            <div class="mdc-dialog__scrim"></div>
        </div>
        </div>

<script type="text/javascript">

    var favCallback = null;

    function showFavPopupAndReload()
    {
        showFavPopup (function () {
            window.location.reload();
        })
    }

    function showFavPopup (callbackFn)
    {
        favCallback = callbackFn;
        $ ('#' + registry.activePage.attr('id') + ' .fav-popup').show ();
    }

    function favConfirm (confirm, favConfirmCallback)
    {
        var postData = 'confirm=' + confirm + '&csrf_token=' + $('#' + registry.activePage.attr('id')  + ' .fav-popup input[name="csrf_token"]').val() + '';
        
        $.ajax ({
            type: "POST",
            url: "https://www.jobs.bg/fav_consent.php",
            data: postData,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (response) {
                if (response.error && response.error == 'csrf') {
                    $('#csrfErrorModal').show();
                    if (response.csrf) {
                        $('#' + registry.activePage.attr('id')  + ' input[name="csrf_token"]').val(response.csrf);
                    }
                }
                else {
                    if (favConfirmCallback) {
                        favConfirmCallback ();
                    }
                    else if (favCallback) {
                        favCallback (confirm, response);
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>

                        document.addEventListener('jQueryReady', function () {

<script type="text/javascript">

    function openJ2EBottomUp()
    {
        $('#subscriptionPromoContainer').addClass('bottom-sheet-show');
    }

    function closeJ2EBottomUp()
    {
        $('#subscriptionPromoContainer').removeClass('bottom-sheet-show');
        $('#j2ePromoEmailInput').val('').blur();
        $('#subscriptionPromoContainer .error').hide();
    }

    function subscribeFromJ2EPromo(btn)
    {
        var emailInput = $('#j2ePromoEmailInput');
        var serializedData = $('#chipForm').serialize () + '&csrf_token=' + encodeURIComponent($('#j2ePromoCSRFInput').val()) + '&subscribe=1' + '';

        if (emailInput.length) {
            serializedData += '&email=' + encodeURIComponent(emailInput.val ());
        }

        btn.hide ();
        $('#subscriptionPromoContainer .error').hide();

        $.ajax ({
            url: 'https://www.jobs.bg/jobs2email_subscribe.php',
            method: 'POST',
            data: serializedData,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (response) {
                if (response.error) {
                    btn.show();
                    if (response.error == 'email') {
                        $("#subscriptionPromoContainer .mdc-text-field").addClass('mdc-text-field--invalid');
                        $('#subscriptionPromoContainer .error').show();
                    }
                    else if (response.error == 'csrf') {
                        openCSRFErrorModal ();
                        if (response.csrf) {
                            $('#j2ePromoCSRFInput').val(response.csrf);
                        }
                    }
                }
                else if (response.html) {
                    closeJ2EBottomUp();
                    $('#j2eSubscriptionPromo').closest('.promo-container').hide();
                    showSnackbarStatus(response.html);
                }
            }
        });
    }

</script>

	
		<script type="application/javascript">

			function ajaxBackToList ()
			{
				$ ('#sendCVPage').remove();

								if (typeof (statsVersion3) != "function") {
					$.getScript( "https://static.jobs.bg/mobile/assets/js/stats.1258d1a3c8397a57ae35.js", function() {
						try {
							statsAdd ('site=jobs.bg&object_id=1&object_type_id=11&action=view&ref=');
						}catch(err) {}
					});
				}
				else {
					try {
						statsAdd ('site=jobs.bg&object_id=1&object_type_id=11&action=view&ref=');
					}catch(err) {}
				}
				
				//loadMetaInfo ();

				if (typeof initStickyContainer !== 'undefined') {
                    initStickyContainer();
                }
			}

			function removeURLParameter (url, parameter)
			{
				var urlparts= url.split ('?');
				if (urlparts.length >= 2) {

					var prefix = encodeURIComponent (parameter) + '=';
					var pars = urlparts [1].split (/[&;]/g);

					for (var i= pars.length; i-- > 0;) {
						if (pars [i].lastIndexOf (prefix, 0) !== -1) {
							pars.splice (i, 1);
						}
					}

					url = urlparts [0]+'?'+pars.join ('&');
					return url;
				}
				else {
					return url;
				}
			}

			var pageDataList = null;

			function countTotal ()
			{
				$.ajax ({
					url: 'https://www.jobs.bg/front_job_search.php?subm=1&keywords%5B0%5D=python&count=1',
					success: function (result) {
						var old = parseInt ($ ('.milestone-total').html());
						result = parseInt (result);
						if (result != old) {
							$ ('.milestone-total').html (result);
							if (pageDataList) {
								pageDataList.end = null;
							}
						}
					}
				});
			}

			function initScrollableList ()
			{
				var url = removeURLParameter ('https://www.jobs.bg/front_job_search.php?subm=1&keywords%5B0%5D=python', 'page');
				url += (url.lastIndexOf ('?') !== -1) ? '&' : '?';

				pageDataList = new Scrollable();
				pageDataList.container = 'listContainer';
				pageDataList.url = url;
				pageDataList.initialPage = '1';
				pageDataList.LIST_LIFETIME = 3600;
				pageDataList.possibleEnd = null;
				pageDataList.initIntersectionObserver();

								pageDataList.needLogos = $(window).width() > 980;
								if (pageDataList.needLogos) {
                    pageDataList.loadLogos(1);
                }

				
				$(window)
					.off('scrollstop')
					.on('scrollstop', function () {
						if (registry.activePage.attr('id') == 'listPage') {
														pageDataList.mileStoneHandle ();
							var currentPadding = parseInt($('#listContainer').css('padding-top').replace("px", ""));
							if (currentPadding > 0 && $(window).scrollTop() < currentPadding) {
								pageDataList.ignoreScrollEvents = true;
								setTimeout(function () {
									$(window).scrollTop(currentPadding);
									pageDataList.ignoreScrollEvents = false;
								});
							}
                            var scrollUpFabBtn = $('.scroll-up-fab');
                            if (scrollUpFabBtn.length) {
                                if ($(window).scrollTop() > 300) {
                                    scrollUpFabBtn.show('fast');
                                }
                                else {
                                    scrollUpFabBtn.hide('fast');
                                }
                            }
						}
					});
			}

			document.addEventListener('jQueryReady', function () {
				$.getScript("https://static.jobs.bg/mobile/assets/js/scrollable.fe6006bc30ece0b97222.js", function() {
					try {
						initScrollableList ();
					}catch(err) {}
				});

				
                if (registry.showVacationPopup) {
                    $ ('#vacationMessage').show ();
                    registry.showVacationPopup = false;
                }

				document.removeEventListener('jQueryReady', arguments.callee);
			});

		</script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
            function openCSRFErrorModal ()
            {
                $('.csrf-error-modal', registry.activePage).show();
            }

            function closeCSRFErrorModal (args)
            {
                                $(args._this).closest('.csrf-error-modal').hide();
            }

            if (!navigator.cookieEnabled) {
                document.addEventListener('jQueryReady', function () {
                    $('.csrf-error-modal-message', registry.activePage).html('Вероятно Вашият браузър не поддържа бисквити. За да ползвате тази функционалност, е нeoбходимо да използвате браузър с включени бисквити.');
                    $('.csrf-error-modal-btn', registry.activePage).html('Затвори');
                    document.removeEventListener('jQueryReady', arguments.callee);
                });
            }
        </script>
    	        <script type="text/javascript">

            document.addEventListener('jQueryReady', function () {
                var page = $('.page.active');
                if (page.length) {
                    fixSpaLinks(page);
                                    }
                document.removeEventListener('jQueryReady', arguments.callee);
            });

            var event;
            if (typeof(Event) === 'function') {
                event = new Event('jQueryReady');
            }
            else {
                event = document.createEvent('Event');
                event.initEvent('jQueryReady', false, true);
            }

            if (typeof $ === 'undefined') {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
                    document.dispatchEvent(event);
                });
            } else {
                document.dispatchEvent(event);
            }
        </script>
